# SkillForge Backlog

> Single source of truth for all work items: bugs, enhancements, and tech debt.
> Spec files in `docs/specs/` describe the *what* and *how*. This file tracks the *what's-next* and *what's-done*.

## Rules
- **IDs are immutable.** Once assigned, a B-### or E-### never changes, never gets reused.
- **One row per item.** Don't split, don't merge. Spawn a new ID if scope splinters.
- **Status is the only field Claude Code may flip autonomously** (ЁЯФ┤ тЖТ ЁЯЯб тЖТ тЬЕ). All other fields require human edit.
- **Closing an item:** status тЖТ тЬЕ + append a one-liner to Notes: `closed by <commit-sha> on <YYYY-MM-DD>`.
- **Priority is a product decision.** Set by Dhamo only.
- **Spec column is the on-disk path** (`docs/specs/phase-N/NN-name.md`). Empty if no spec exists yet тАФ create one before implementation.

## Status legend
- ЁЯФ┤ Pending (not started)
- ЁЯЯб In progress / partial / blocked
- тЬЕ Done
- тЪк Won't do / deferred indefinitely
- ЁЯЯж Back-burner тАФ scoped out, awaiting activation gate (e.g., telemetry threshold). Not worked on until the gate trips.

## Priority legend
- **P0** тАФ broken in production, blocking users, blocking next milestone
- **P1** тАФ committed for this phase
- **P2** тАФ wanted, not committed
- **P3** тАФ someday / nice-to-have

---

| B-014 | ats-scanner | Section rewrite path missing `thinking_budget` тЖТ Gemini 2.5 Pro MAX_TOKENS тЖТ 502 "Regenerate with Resume" | P0 | тЬЕ | docs/specs/phase-5/51-ai-rewrite-section-preservation.md | (from 2026-04-21 E2E bug diagnosis) | Closed 2026-04-21 by `067c232`. Root cause: `gpt_service.py:380-387` (chunked `_rewrite_one_section`) and `:615-622` (per-section endpoint `generate_section_rewrite`) called `generate_for_task(task="resume_rewrite_section", max_tokens=SECTION_MAX_TOKENS=2500, ...)` without `thinking_budget`, so Gemini 2.5 Pro's reasoning tier consumed ~2497 tokens on internal thinking, hit `FinishReason.MAX_TOKENS`, and returned empty text тЖТ `RewriteError("rewrite_parse_error")` тЖТ HTTP 502. The full-rewrite fallback at `:487-495` already passed `thinking_budget=FULL_REWRITE_THINKING_BUDGET` correctly тАФ the section path was the only omission. Fix: added `SECTION_THINKING_BUDGET = 800` constant, bumped `SECTION_MAX_TOKENS = 2500 тЖТ 4000` for headroom, passed `thinking_budget=SECTION_THINKING_BUDGET` to both section call sites. Regression tests in `tests/services/test_resume_rewrite.py` (+3): guard section-call signature contains `thinking_budget`, guard per-section endpoint same, guard constant-level headroom invariant (`SECTION_MAX_TOKENS >= 2 * SECTION_THINKING_BUDGET`). Diagnosis: `docs/status/E2E-BUG-DIAGNOSIS-2026-04-21.md` ┬зBug (a) + `backend.log:149-178` (thoughts_token_count=2497, max_tokens=2500). |

| B-021 | interview | Cover letter prompt always receives "your company" тАФ `extract_job_requirements` never populates `company_name` | P2 | тЬЕ | | (from 2026-04-22 bug report тАФ surfaced as "Conversational tone regen doesn't pull JD company details") | Closed 2026-04-22 by `e7c6d73`. Shipped: `nlp.py` gains heuristic `_extract_company_name(jd_text) -> str | None` using 5 high-precision regex patterns (`About X:` / `About X тАФ`, `Join [the] X team/as/in`, `X is hiring/looking for/seeking`, `at X.` position anchor, `Company: X` line). `extract_job_requirements` now returns `"company_name": str | None` in its dict тАФ two live consumers pick it up automatically: `gpt_service.generate_cover_letter` prompt reads it instead of defaulting to "your company", and `api/routes/analyze.py` tracker autopopulate writes real company names instead of "Unknown Company". Low-confidence JDs return None, and both consumer fallbacks ("your company" / "Unknown Company") remain intact for that case тАФ silent misses are strictly better than false positives ending up in the prompt. `_COMPANY_TOKEN` uses `[ \t]+` (not `\s+`) between Title-Case words to prevent the regex backtracking across blank lines and absorbing a preceding headline. Tone-agnostic root cause; three-tone parametrized test guards tone invariance. Tests: BE +19 (9 happy-path parametrized extractor cases, 4 None-fallback cases, 3 tone ├Ч company-flows-into-prompt, 1 fallback-preserved, 1 shape-stability, 1 populated end-to-end). No new endpoint, no schema change, no LLM call. **Deliberately NOT in scope:** FE `CoverLetterRequest.company_name` override field (user-confirmed company name), LLM-based extraction, batch-backfill of existing "Unknown Company" tracker rows. | `hirelens-backend/app/services/nlp.py::extract_job_requirements` returns `required_skills, preferred_skills, all_skills, job_title, seniority_level, responsibilities` тАФ no `company_name`. Three consumers read `jd_requirements.get("company_name")` and all fall through to placeholder: `gpt_service.py:658` тЖТ `"your company"` (cover-letter prompt, the bug surface), `api/routes/analyze.py:209` тЖТ `"Unknown Company"` (tracker autopopulate rows), `ai_service.py:148` (dead code тАФ S47-defer, spec #52 ┬з2). **Tone-agnostic**: bug surfaces most on Conversational because formal tones mask "your company" with ceremonial language; Conversational expects personable specificity. **Fix shape:** add a heuristic `_extract_company_name(jd_text)` to `nlp.py` (consistent with `_detect_seniority` / `_extract_responsibilities` regex approach); `extract_job_requirements` includes `"company_name": <str | None>` in its return dict. Fallback "your company" / "Unknown Company" strings in consumers remain for the low-confidence case тАФ benign when extraction misses. Two live consumers improve simultaneously. No new endpoint, no schema change, no new LLM call. Tests: `nlp.py` unit tests for the extractor across common JD shapes; cover-letter service test that end-to-end the prompt receives the extracted name instead of "your company" when the JD contains a known-pattern company mention. |

| B-026 | design-system | Native `<input type="date">` calendar icon invisible on dark themes тАФ `color-scheme` never set on `:root` | P2 | тЬЕ | | (from 2026-04-22 bug report тАФ PersonaPicker date field on "What brings you to SkillForge?" page) | Closed 2026-04-22 by `a436364`. Root cause: the app has 3 themes applied via CSS variables (`applyTheme` in `src/styles/design-tokens.ts:319-325`) but never sets the browser's `color-scheme` property on the theme-target element. Browsers render native `<input type="date">` calendar icons + scrollbars + number spinners using the effective `color-scheme` (defaults to `light`), so on Dark and Midnight Blue themes the calendar icon is dark-grey on dark background тАФ effectively invisible. Not scoped to PersonaPicker; the issue affects every native form control app-wide. **Fix shape (design-system-level, zero per-component edits):** extended the `Theme` interface with `colorScheme: 'dark' | 'light'`; declared it per-theme (`dark: 'dark'`, `midnight-blue: 'dark'`, `light: 'light'`); made `applyTheme` also set `el.style.colorScheme = theme.colorScheme`. Every native picker/scrollbar/spinner now renders in sympathy with the active theme, including after runtime theme switches. No CSS-file edits, no Tailwind config change, no `color-scheme` utility sprinkled through components. **Not a retrofit or new feature тАФ R14 exception (b) pure bug fix.** Tests: FE 214 unchanged (visual behavior of native browser chrome isn't unit-test surface; `tsc --noEmit` clean confirms the interface extension). **Deliberately NOT in scope:** broader cross-browser date-picker redesign (deferred тАФ native picker is the established UX per spec #53 LD-2), custom-theming of `::-webkit-calendar-picker-indicator` beyond what `color-scheme` provides, `meta[name="color-scheme"]` setting for initial-paint behavior (would be a micro-optimization). |

| B-024 | interview | Cover letter and tracker autopopulate render "your company" / "Unknown Company" for valid JDs тАФ `_extract_company_name` regex recall gap | P1 | тЬЕ | | (from 2026-04-22 bug report with artifact тАФ JPMorgan JD) | Closed 2026-04-22 by `50e3c3c`. Root cause: B-021's `_extract_company_name` used 5 high-precision regex patterns with intentionally narrow recall (precision-first). Real JDs in shapes not covered by the patterns тАФ including the JPMorgan Chase & Co. JD used in the bug repro, which uses a standalone-header-line shape (`"JPMorgan Chase & Co.\n"`) with no `About X:` / `Join X` / `X is hiring` anchor тАФ returned None and the cover-letter prompt fell through to `"your company"`, tracker autopopulate to `"Unknown Company"`. Verified against the JPMorgan JD: 0 of 5 patterns matched. **Three-layer design shipped (layers 1 + 3):** (1) LLM primary тАФ new `company_name_extraction` task on FAST tier (`gemini-2.0-flash` default) in `llm_router.py`; prompt explicitly instructs null-on-unclear, rejects role-title / aggregator responses, preserves verbatim capitalization. (2) Manual user entry on null тАФ **deferred to B-025** (separate spec required). (3) Existing `"your company"` / `"Unknown Company"` consumer fallback preserved for the null case. **Orchestrator policy** (`nlp.py::_extract_company_name`): LLM raises (network/quota/config) тЖТ regex fallback (preserves pre-B-024 behavior on transient outages); LLM returns null (valid "unclear" judgment) тЖТ return None (do NOT re-try regex тАФ null is data, not error); LLM returns string тЖТ aggregator deny-list backstop (`{linkedin, indeed, glassdoor, monster, ziprecruiter, careerbuilder, dice, wellfound, angellist, simplyhired}`), 100-char length cap, return. **Role-title rejection** enforced in the LLM prompt (not server-side) per the "STOP if validator gets more complex than deny-list" guard тАФ cleaner boundary and avoids collision with `extract_job_requirements`'s buggy first-line `job_title` heuristic. Both live consumers inherit the fix transparently (cover-letter prompt + `api/routes/analyze.py` tracker autopopulate). **Cost impact:** adds one Flash call (~1k input + ~50 output tokens тЙИ $0.00014) per `extract_job_requirements` invocation, which fires once per ATS scan and once per cover-letter generation. Negligible at current scale (~$1.40/mo per 10k scans). **Latency impact:** +500-800ms per scan (Flash median) тАФ acceptable trade-off under precision-first policy. Tests: BE +10 (`test_nlp.py`): positive (JPMorgan JD, LLM mocked to return verbatim); null тЖТ None without regex fallback; aggregator rejection (case-sensitive + case-insensitive); empty-string output тЖТ None; malformed JSON тЖТ None (treated as null, not infra failure); infra-failure тЖТ regex-fallback happy; infra-failure + regex-miss тЖТ None; empty-JD short-circuit before LLM call; 100-char length cap. Existing B-021 9-positive + 4-negative parametrized tests renamed to target `_extract_company_name_regex` directly so fallback path stays covered independently. End-to-end `extract_job_requirements` tests now mock the LLM explicitly. **Deliberately NOT in scope:** B-025 layer 2 (manual entry UI), LLM prompt tuning for better recall, role-title server-side rejection (prompt-enforced), tracker backfill of existing "Unknown Company" rows. **D-016 stays ЁЯЯб open** тАФ unrelated latent gap (cover-letter `response_schema` never plumbed). |
| B-023 | interview | Cover letter signature renders "KEY ACHIEVEMENTS" (or other all-caps section header) тАФ `_extract_candidate_name` false-positive matches all-caps resume headers | P1 | тЬЕ | | (from 2026-04-22 bug report with artifact) | Closed 2026-04-22 by `79f76b4`. Root cause: `gpt_service.py::_extract_candidate_name` walked the first 10 resume lines and accepted any 2тАУ4-token line where every token matched `^[A-Z][A-Za-z.'-]+$` тАФ that regex silently accepts all-uppercase tokens (`"KEY"`, `"ACHIEVEMENTS"`) because `[A-Za-z]+` allows uppercase. When the candidate's real name was not in the first 10 lines, the helper returned a section header instead. The header was then interpolated into the cover-letter prompt as the signature field, the LLM dutifully echoed it, and `_join_cover_letter` rendered "Sincerely,\nKEY ACHIEVEMENTS" unchanged. **NOT a schema-enforcement issue** тАФ the LLM output was structurally valid JSON; the prompt was feeding it a poisoned candidate_name. D-016 (missing `response_schema`) stays ЁЯЯб open as a separate latent defense-in-depth gap; neither B-023 nor B-024 closes it. **Fix shape:** self-documenting early-return guard тАФ before the token-regex check, skip any line that is pure-uppercase (`line == line.upper()` after confirming at least one letter is present, so digit/punct-only lines fall through to the existing guards). Human names capitalize the first letter per token, not every letter тАФ no legitimate candidate-name line is pure-uppercase. Tests: BE +12 (`test_cover_letter_format.py`): 6 parametrized positives (`"Jordan Doe"`, `"Dhamo Sankaran"`, `"Mary-Kate O'Neill"`, `"Alice Johnson"`, `"Dr. Alice Johnson"`, `"Jean-Luc Picard"`) + 4 parametrized all-caps negatives (`"KEY ACHIEVEMENTS"`, `"PROFESSIONAL SUMMARY"`, `"WORK EXPERIENCE"`, `"EDUCATION"`) + 1 skips-header-finds-real-name-below + 1 blank-resume fallback. **Deliberately NOT in scope:** B-024 (separate row, on hold for JD text) тАФ company-name regex recall gap that produces the "your company" leak surfaced in the same artifact. Root causes do not overlap; schema enforcement would not close either. |
| B-022 | ats-scanner | Analysis Results (`generate_job_fit_explanation`) routed via fast tier тАФ reasoning quality lags rest of Analysis Results surface | P2 | тЬЕ | | (from 2026-04-22 post-E2E handoff) | Closed 2026-04-22 by `fa1871e`. | E-046 | tracker | Real-time recruiter-call AI copilot | P3 | ЁЯЯж | | (from 2026-04-23 product-scope conversation) | **DO-NOT-BUILD (permanent rejection).** Explicit rejection row exists so future sessions do not re-litigate this scope. **Rationale:** (a) TOS-violation surface on target employers' interview processes (recording / AI-listening on a recruiter call without explicit consent violates most major employers' interview conduct policies and some states' one-party-recording-law liability frameworks); (b) one-party-recording-law liability varies by jurisdiction (California / Illinois / Maryland + several others require two-party consent тАФ a nationwide product cannot quietly assume one-party); (c) commoditized LLM-wrapper space тАФ no moat extension from current study-loop differentiation; (d) support burden for the 5% of users who'd use it outweighs revenue upside at our scale. **No gate.
